{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 
 示例：指定时空guid、业务物对象id

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID; //指定时空guid
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::ID; //指定对象id

//指定第一个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);

//指定第二个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);

condition["objects"] = objects;
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$guid","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 

# 3.4.4.4. 查询指定模型的对象

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL, /*查找模式*/
 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
spaceTimeNames:string[],
spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[], 
/*选填*/spaceTimeScope:int32, /*查询的时空范围设置，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeScope*/ 
 
modelGUID:string, //modelGUID支持空串，代表不限模型；
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [],
/*选填*/filter:string, 
 
returnFields:string[],
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/
 
/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string, /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
/*选填*/forLock:int32 /*锁定配置，不支持单/多灵敏时序物对象*/
}
**脚本示例1：**查询本时空/数据区下指定模型的对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 查找数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["filter"] = "$name == \"物料G30\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"}; // 返回字段
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
**脚本示例2：**查询指定时空下指定模型的对象

#### 3.4.4.4. 查询指定模型的对象

# 3.4.4.5. 查询指定多个拷贝的对象

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST, /*查找模式*/ 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
spaceTimeNames:string[],
spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[], 
/*选填*/spaceTimeScope:int32, /*查询的时空范围设置，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeScope*/
 
copyGUIDs:string[],
 
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [], 
returnFields:string[],
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
**脚本示例1：**查询当前时空/数据区下指定拷贝的对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参

stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 查找数据区
condition["copyGUIDs"] = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
**脚本示例2：**查询指定时空下指定拷贝的对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;

condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1","gc2"};
condition["copyGUIDs"] = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;

 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 3.4.4.5. 查询指定多个拷贝的对象

 condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST, /*查找模式*/ 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
spaceTimeNames:string[],
spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[], 
/*选填*/spaceTimeScope:int32, /*查询的时空范围设置，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeScope*/
 
copyGUIDs:string[],
 
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap<var>[], 
returnFields:string[],
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap<var>[], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap<var>[], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 
 脚本示例1： 查询当前时空/数据区下指定拷贝的对象

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 查找数据区
condition["copyGUIDs"] = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 
 脚本示例2： 查询指定时空下指定拷贝的对象

# 3.4.4.6. 查询指定父对象的子对象（单灵敏时序物/多灵敏时序物/业务物/组织/岗位/业务事/时序事）

注意事项：岗位的父是组织，如果查询岗位对象，则startCondition的条件是针对组织对象的；
单灵敏时序物对象、多灵敏时序物对象的父是业务物，如果查询单灵敏时序物对象、多灵敏时序物对象，则startCondition的条件是针对业务物对象的；

#### 3.4.4.6. 查询指定父对象的子对象（单灵敏时序物/多灵敏时序物/业务物/组织/岗位/业务事/时序事）

 注意事项：岗位的父是组织，如果查询岗位对象，则startCondition的条件是针对组织对象的；
单灵敏时序物对象、多灵敏时序物对象的父是业务物，如果查询单灵敏时序物对象、多灵敏时序物对象，则startCondition的条件是针对业务物对象的；

# 3.4.4.6.1. 查询所有子对象

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始父对象节点条件
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST; 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL, /*子对象的查找模式*/
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/ 

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
**脚本示例1：** 查询指定时空下指定父对象的所有子对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name、父对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
示例：指定时空guid、父对象id
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;

object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 3.4.4.6.1. 查询所有子对象 
 condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始父对象节点条件
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST; 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL, /*子对象的查找模式*/
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap<var>[],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap<var>[], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap<var>[], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/ 

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 
 脚本示例1： 查询指定时空下指定父对象的所有子对象

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 示例：指定时空name、父对象name

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap<var> startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 
 示例：指定时空guid、父对象id

{

# 3.4.4.6.2. 查询子对象中，指定模型的对象

mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始父对象节点条件
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:

/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,

　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL, /*子对象的查找模式*/
modelGUID:string,
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
**脚本示例1：** 查询指定时空下指定对象的指定模型的子对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name、父对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询指定模型的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{

 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap<var> startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::ID;

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询指定模型的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 

# 3.4.4.7. 查询指定祖先对象的后代对象（业务物/组织/时序事/业务事）

注意事项：
对象的祖先后代查询支持返回以下特殊字段：
$distance, （距离）
$startName/$startAlias/$startGUID/$startID, （起始对象信息，取决于startCondition中的objectIdentifierType）

#### 3.4.4.7. 查询指定祖先对象的后代对象（业务物/组织/时序事/业务事）

 注意事项：

 对象的祖先后代查询支持返回以下特殊字段：

 $distance, （距离）

 $startName/$startAlias/$startGUID/$startID, （起始对象信息，取决于startCondition中的objectIdentifierType）

# 3.4.4.7.1. 查询所有后代对象

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始祖先对象节点条件
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL, /*后代对象的查找模式*/
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/
 
/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
**脚本示例1：** 查询指定时空下指定对象的所有后代对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name、对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的后代对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2

/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap<var>[], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 
 脚本示例1： 查询指定时空下指定对象的所有后代对象

# 3.4.4.7.2. 查询后代对象中，指定模型的对象

condition:{
　 mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始祖先对象节点条件
 {

objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,

　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},

modelGUID:string,
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap [],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/

/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/

}
**脚本示例1：** 查询指定时空下指定对象的指定模型的后代对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name、对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询指定模型的后代对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 3.4.4.7.2. 查询后代对象中，指定模型的对象 
 condition:{
　 mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT, /*查找模式*/
 
startCondition: //起始祖先对象节点条件
 { 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL, /*后代对象的查找模式*/
modelGUID:string,
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringMap<var>[],
/*选填*/filter:string,　
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段*/
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap<var>[], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap<var>[], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/

/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 
 脚本示例1： 查询指定时空下指定对象的指定模型的后代对象

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 示例：指定时空name、对象name

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::DESCENDANT; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap<var> startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询指定模型的后代对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

# 3.4.4.8. 查询指定的组织对象下符合条件的人员对象(人员)

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::ORG_CONDITION, /*查找模式*/
 
orgCondition:
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32, /*组织下人员的查找模式，支持的查找模式：::OBJECT_ALL、::OBJECT_BY_MODEL*/
 //人员的查找模式的参数，
 
//mainMode:int32==Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL时有效的参数-start1: //查找组织下的所有人员
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringmap [],
/*选填*/filter:string, //-end1 
 
//mainMode:int32==Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL时有效的参数-start2: //查找组织下指定模型的人员
modelGUID:string,
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringmap [],
/*选填*/filter:string, //-end2
 
returnFields:string[],
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap [], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap [], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/
 
/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
**脚本示例1：** 查询指定时空下指定组织下的人员对象
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
示例：指定时空name、组织name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap orgCondition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::ORG_CONDITION; // 查找模式
// 组织对象的筛选
orgCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
orgCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
orgCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"组织对象11","组织对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"组织对象21","组织对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

orgCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询组织下所有的人员对象
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询组织下指定模型的人员对象
condition.clear();
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
示例：指定时空guid、组织id

orgCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};

//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};

// 查询组织下所有的人员对象

condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询组织下指定模型的人员对象
condition.clear();
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 3.4.4.8. 查询指定的组织对象下符合条件的人员对象(人员)

 condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::ORG_CONDITION, /*查找模式*/
 
orgCondition:
{ 
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[] //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}] //-end2
},
 
mainMode:int32, /*组织下人员的查找模式，支持的查找模式：::OBJECT_ALL、::OBJECT_BY_MODEL*/
 //人员的查找模式的参数，
 
//mainMode:int32==Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL时有效的参数-start1: //查找组织下的所有人员
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringmap<var>[],
/*选填*/filter:string, //-end1 
 
//mainMode:int32==Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL时有效的参数-start2: //查找组织下指定模型的人员
modelGUID:string,
/*选填*/derivedFields:stringmap<var>[],
/*选填*/filter:string, //-end2
 
returnFields:string[],
 
/*选填*/groupFields:string[], /*分组参数*/
/*选填*/aggregates:stringMap<var>[], /*聚合参数*/
/*选填*/postFilter:string, /*分组、聚合过滤参数*/
/*选填*/distinct:bool, /*去重参数，=true去重，默认不去重*/
/*选填*/orders:stringMap<var>[], /*排序参数，支持升序，降序*/
/*选填*/offset:int32, /*分页参数，起始行数，最小为1，默认1*/
/*选填*/limit:int32, /*分页参数，返回数据行数，最小为1，默认20000*/
 
/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 
 脚本示例1： 查询指定时空下指定组织下的人员对象

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 示例：指定时空name、组织name

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var> orgCondition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::ORG_CONDITION; // 查找模式
// 组织对象的筛选
orgCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
orgCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
orgCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"组织对象11","组织对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"组织对象21","组织对象22"};
objects.push(new object);

orgCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询组织下所有的人员对象
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询组织下指定模型的人员对象
condition.clear();
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 
 示例：指定时空guid、组织id

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型
// 入参

orgCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
orgCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::ID;

object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);

orgCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询组织下所有的人员对象
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询组织下指定模型的人员对象
condition.clear();
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 

# 3.4.4.9. 查询指定的多个对象的列表属性

#### 3.4.4.9. 查询指定的多个对象的列表属性

# 3.4.4.9.1. 查询指定的多个对象的列表属性：组织岗位（type=人员对象）、外键（type=业务事对象）、唯一索引（type=业务事对象）

condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST, 
dataField:string, /* 字段名称，此处为列表属性字段 */
 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[], //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}], //-end2
 
/*选填*/duplicationDealMode:int32,/*根据名称查询对象时，重名时的处理模式，
 详见枚举Enum_Rt_DuplicationDealMode*/

/*选填*/filter:string, /*过滤列表属性的字段*/
 
returnFields:string[], /*返回字段，支持列表属性元素的字段），
　 支持$objectName/$objectAlias/$objectGUID/$objectID之一（由objectIdentifierType决定）*/
/*选填*/returnMode:int32, /*返回模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_ReturnMode*/
dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}

 3.4.4.9.1. 查询指定的多个对象的列表属性：组织岗位（type=人员对象）、外键（type=业务事对象）、唯一索引（type=业务事对象） 
 condition:{
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST, 
dataField:string, /* 字段名称，此处为列表属性字段 */
 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[], //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}], //-end2

 详见枚举Enum_Rt_DuplicationDealMode*/

　 支持$objectName/$objectAlias/$objectGUID/$objectID之一（由objectIdentifierType决定）*/

dataSetName:string /*数据集名称，命名规则同queryjoin的asName，非展开查询时必填*/
}
 

# 3.4.5. 订阅

### 3.4.5. 订阅

# 3.4.5.1. 订阅综述

**Result Subscribe(stringMap\ param,stringMap\ input,stringMap\ &output)**
**功能描述：**订阅对象的事件。
**param有效参数:**
cloudID
int32
云ID
是

areaID
int32
数据区ID
是

type
int32
数据类型
是

callbackFuncName
string
异步回调函数名称
是

transactionID
uint64
事务ID。订阅不支持事务，该参数无效
否
0
timeout
int32
超时时间
否
10000
translateMode
int32
翻译模式，详见枚举Enum_TranslateMode；该参数仅对StringEx成员有效[开发中，尚未提供]
否
NO_TRANSLATION
language
string
目标语言类型，该参数仅对StringEx成员有效[开发中，尚未提供]
否
同仓库的语言类型（localeLanguage）
**input有效参数:**
conditions
stringMap\ []
订阅参数配置，多个map组成，输入参数conditions支持多个condition，每个condition的参数结构都可以不同，互不影响；
单个condition支持的结构参见各个功能点章节；
是

**output参数:**
subscribeIDs
uint32[]
订阅ID数组，和conditions顺序对应
errorCodes
int32[]
结果码集合，和conditions顺序对应
errorCodeExs
stringMap\ []
子结果码集合，为空或和conditions顺序对应
**错误码:**
参见《实时库错误码表》
**脚本示例：**
参见各个功能点章节

# 3.4.5.2. 订阅回调

Dataset callback
1、创建/删除/移入时空/移出时空事件数据集结构：
数据集列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string
2、修改事件数据集结构：
1、业务物/组织/岗位/人员对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,stringMap 

2、单灵敏时序物对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$value,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,
$old_value,$old_timeStamp,$old_qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,var,int64,int32,
var,int64,int32,stringMap 
--VTQ的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$value,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,
$old_value,$old_timeStamp,$old_qualityStamp
--其他普通字段的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues

3、多灵敏时序物对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,int64,int32,stringMap 
--灵敏字段（时间、质量、灵敏成员）的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
--其他普通字段的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues
注意事项：
建议用户读取订阅回调数据集中的数据时，通过数据集列名读取列，而不是通过列号，以应对产品版本升级的情况；

#### 3.4.5.2. 订阅回调

 Dataset callback

 1、创建/删除/移入时空/移出时空事件数据集结构：

 数据集列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string
 
 2、修改事件数据集结构：

 1、业务物/组织/岗位/人员对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,stringMap<var> 

2、单灵敏时序物对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$value,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,
$old_value,$old_timeStamp,$old_qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,var,int64,int32,
var,int64,int32,stringMap<var>
--VTQ的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$value,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,
$old_value,$old_timeStamp,$old_qualityStamp
--其他普通字段的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues

3、多灵敏时序物对象：
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
列类型：int32,int32,string,uint64,string,string,int64,int32,stringMap<var>
--灵敏字段（时间、质量、灵敏成员）的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$timeStamp,$qualityStamp,$updateFieldValues
--其他普通字段的修改事件有效字段：（其他字段的值为空或不可靠）
列名：$type,$eventType,$spaceTimeGUID,$id,$name,$guid,$updateFieldValues
 
 注意事项：

 建议用户读取订阅回调数据集中的数据时，通过数据集列名读取列，而不是通过列号，以应对产品版本升级的情况；

# 3.4.5.3. 订阅对象的多种事件类型

创建事件：要求数据创建后满足时空条件并满足mode筛选条件；
删除事件：要求数据删除前满足时空条件并满足mode筛选条件；
移入时空事件：要求对象修改前不位于订阅时空，修改后位于订阅时空并满足mode筛选条件，修改时空（$spaceTimeGUID）时触发；
移出时空事件：要求对象修改前位于订阅时空并满足mode筛选条件，修改后不再位于订阅时空，修改时空（$spaceTimeGUID）时触发； 

#### 3.4.5.3. 订阅对象的多种事件类型

 创建事件：要求数据创建后满足时空条件并满足mode筛选条件；

 删除事件：要求数据删除前满足时空条件并满足mode筛选条件；

 移入时空事件：要求对象修改前不位于订阅时空，修改后位于订阅时空并满足mode筛选条件，修改时空（$spaceTimeGUID）时触发；

 移出时空事件：要求对象修改前位于订阅时空并满足mode筛选条件，修改后不再位于订阅时空，修改时空（$spaceTimeGUID）时触发； 

# 3.4.5.3.1. 订阅指定对象的删除事件

通过name访问时，如果时空内存在重名，操作失败。
condition:{
subscribeName:string,//订阅名称
/*选填*/pubConfig:stringMap ,//订阅发布配置
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST,
 
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[], //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
 objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeAlias:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
　aliases:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}], //-end2
 
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES, 
eventTypes:int32[]
}
**脚本示例1：** 订阅当前时空/数据区下指定对象的删除事件
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode、Enum_Rt_EventType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback
示例：指定对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
示例：指定对象guid
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;

condition["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};

else

 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
**脚本示例2：** 订阅指定时空下指定对象的删除事件
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode、Enum_Rt_EventType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode、Enum_Rt_EventType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区

else

condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

 3.4.5.3.2. 订阅指定模型的对象的创建、删除、移入时空、移出时空事件 
 condition:{
subscribeName:string, //订阅名称
/*选填*/pubConfig:stringMap<var>, //订阅发布配置
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL,
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, /*时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode*/
 
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
spaceTimeNames:string[],
spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[], 
 
modelGUID:string,
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES, 
eventTypes:int32[],
}
 
 脚本示例1： 订阅当前时空/数据区指定模型的对象的创建、删除、移入时空、移出时空事件

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode、Enum_Rt_EventType，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap<var> pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE, (int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE,(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_IN_SPACETIME, (int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_OUT_SPACETIME};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

# 3.4.5.4. 订阅对象的修改事件(单灵敏时序物/多灵敏时序物/业务物/组织/岗位/人员)

订阅范围内，只要订阅的字段subFields之一发生修改就会触发订阅；
subField不支持列表属性字段；
如果对象修改时，改变了时空，属于时空的移入移出事件，不会进入修改订阅的回调；

#### 3.4.5.4. 订阅对象的修改事件(单灵敏时序物/多灵敏时序物/业务物/组织/岗位/人员)

 订阅范围内，只要订阅的字段subFields之一发生修改就会触发订阅；
subField不支持列表属性字段；
如果对象修改时，改变了时空，属于时空的移入移出事件，不会进入修改订阅的回调；

# 3.4.5.4.1. 订阅指定的对象的修改事件

condition:{
subscribeName:string,//订阅名称
/*选填*/pubConfig:stringMap ,//订阅发布配置
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST,
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, //时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[], //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}], //-end2
 
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS, 
subFields:string[]
}
**脚本示例1：** 订阅当前时空/数据区下指定对象的修改事件
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback
示例：指定对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
示例：指定对象guid

**脚本示例2：** 订阅指定时空下指定对象的修改事件
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback
示例：指定时空name、对象name
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-指定时空
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST2";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
//------指定第一个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
//------指定第二个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc2";
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"}; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
示例：指定时空guid、对象id
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-指定时空
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST2";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::ID;
//------指定第一个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
//------指定第二个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"}; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

 3.4.5.4.1. 订阅指定的对象的修改事件 
 condition:{
subscribeName:string,//订阅名称
/*选填*/pubConfig:stringMap<var>,//订阅发布配置
/*选填*/mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST,
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, //时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode
 
//spaceTimeMode为::CURRENT_SPACETIME（默认模式）或者::ALL_SPACETIME时的有效的参数 -start1:
/*选填*/identifierType:int32, /*当spaceTimeMode为::ALL_SPACETIME时，该值不能为::ALIAS*/
names:string[],
guids:string[], 
ids:uint64[], //-end1

//spaceTimeMode为::SPECIFY_SPACETIME时有效的参数 -start2:
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
/*选填*/objectIdentifierType:int32,
objects: 
　[{ 
 spaceTimeName:string,
　spaceTimeGUID:string,
　spaceTimeID:uint64,
　names:string[],
 guids:string[], 
　ids:uint64[],
　}], //-end2
 
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS, 
subFields:string[]
}
 
 脚本示例1： 订阅当前时空/数据区下指定对象的修改事件

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback

 示例：指定对象name

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap<var> pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
 
 示例：指定对象guid

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称

//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;

 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");

 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);

# 3.4.5.4.2. 订阅指定模型的对象的修改事件

condition:{
subscribeName:string,//订阅名称
/*选填*/pubConfig:stringMap ,//订阅发布配置
mode:int32=Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL,
/*选填*/spaceTimeMode:int32, //时空选择模式，详见枚举Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode
 
spaceTimeIdentifierType:int32,
spaceTimeNames:string[],
spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[],
 
modelGUID:string, 
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS, 
subFields:string[]
}
**脚本示例1：** 订阅当前时空/数据区指定模型的对象的修改事件
前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。
前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

 condition:{

spaceTimeGUIDs:string[],
spaceTimeIDs:uint64[],
 
modelGUID:string, 
cmdCode:int32=Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS, 
subFields:string[]
}
 
 脚本示例1： 订阅当前时空/数据区指定模型的对象的修改事件

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap<var> pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
 
 脚本示例2： 订阅指定时空下指定模型的对象的修改事件

 前置枚举：需要提前在declare中声明枚举Enum_Rt_Type、Enum_Rt_Mode、Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode、Enum_Rt_IdentifierType、Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode，详见《实时库系统枚举》。

 前置功能：需要提前定义回调功能，名称：callbackfunc1，输入参数：dataset callback

 示例：指定时空name

condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1","gc2"};
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 出参

// 订阅对象

{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");

}
else
{

 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
 
 示例：指定时空guid

param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID

condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["spaceTimeGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["spaceTimeIDs"] = {(uint64)18158513697557839872,(uint64)18158513697557839873};

// 出参

// 订阅对象

{

}
else
{
