# 4.5.4.5. 查询指定多个拷贝的对象

// 示例：查询指定多个拷贝下的对象
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
//查找本时空/数据区
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 查找数据区
condition["copyGUIDs"] = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//查找指定时空
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_COPY_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 查找指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1/cj1/cx1","gc1/cj1/cx2"};
//condition["spaceTimeGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["spaceTimeIDs"] = {(uint64)18158513697557839872,(uint64)18158513697557839873};
condition["copyGUIDs"] = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$id","$name","mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{

 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码

 int32[] exErrorCodes;

 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

# 4.5.4.6. 查询指定父对象的子对象

// 示例：查询指定2个父对象的所有子对象
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD; // 查找模式
// 父节点的筛选
stringMap startCondition;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//object["spaceTimeAlias"] = "产线1";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};

objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询指定模型的子对象
condition.clear();
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};

objects.push(new object);

startCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询所有的子对象
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\"";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询指定模型的子对象
condition.clear();
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "$name include \"物料\" && mem1 > 100";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$parentGUID","$id","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");

else
{

# 4.5.4.8. 查询指定的组织对象下的人员对象

// 示例：查询指定2个组织下指定拷贝的人员对象
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap orgCondition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::ORG_CONDITION; // 查找模式
// 组织对象的筛选
orgCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
orgCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
orgCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "jt/gc1";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象31","业务物对象32"};
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "jt/gc2";
//object["spaceTimeAlias"] = "工厂2";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象31","业务物对象32"};
//object["aliases"] = {"车间1","车间2"};
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);

orgCondition["objects"] = objects;

// 查询组织下所有的人员对象
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_ALL; // 查找模式
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询组织下指定模型的人员对象
condition.clear();
condition["orgCondition"] = orgCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL; // 查找模式
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeName","$orgAlias","$name","$id","$mem1"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询对象
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 uint64 idI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 idI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$id");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码

 int32[] exErrorCodes;

# 4.5.5. 订阅对象

### 4.5.5. 订阅对象

# 4.5.5.1. 订阅对象的多种事件类型

#### 4.5.5.1. 订阅对象的多种事件类型

# 4.5.5.1.1. 订阅指定的对象

// 脚本示例：订阅指定对象的删除事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
//condition["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);
//-指定时空
condition.clear();
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST2";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
//------指定第一个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象11","业务物对象12"};
//object["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
//------指定第二个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
object["names"] = {"业务物对象21","业务物对象22"};
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;

//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};

// 脚本示例：订阅指定模型的对象的创建、删除、移入时空、移出时空事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE, (int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE,(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_IN_SPACETIME, (int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_OUT_SPACETIME};
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);
//-指定时空
condition.clear();
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST2";
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; //指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1/cj1/cx1","gc1/cj1/cx2"};
//condition["spaceTimeGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};

condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
 eventTypes = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE, (int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
eventTypes.push((int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_IN_SPACETIME);
eventTypes.push((int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_OUT_SPACETIME);
condition["eventTypes"] = eventTypes; // 事件类型
conditions.push(new condition);

# 4.5.5.1.3. 订阅回调

// 订阅功能回调功能入参声明：Dataset callback

int32 rowLen = callback.rowLength; // 数据集总行数
int32 rowNo = 1; // 数据集行号，这里以一行举例，请视实际情况决定要不要循环处理

int32 type = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$type");
int32 eventType = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$eventType");

if(Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 //业务逻辑
}
else if(Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 //业务逻辑
}
else if(Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_IN_SPACETIME == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 //业务逻辑
}
else if(Enum_Rt_EventType::MOVE_OUT_SPACETIME == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 //业务逻辑
}

 4.5.5.1.3. 订阅回调

int32 rowNo = 1; // 数据集行号，这里以一行举例，请视实际情况决定要不要循环处理

# 4.5.5.2.1. 订阅指定的对象

// 脚本示例：订阅指定对象的修改事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition.clear(); 
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"对象11","对象12"};
//condition["guids"] = {"8B9B07EE-FFA4-4755-9DDA-89E8875D5CF5","06a7f048-c653-4f28-8c6f-d66bfec8f6af"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//-指定时空
condition.clear(); 
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_OBJECT_LIST2";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
//------指定第一个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
object["names"] = {"对象11","对象12"};

//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235556,(uint64)158789545685235557};
objects.push(new object);
//------指定第二个时空内的对象
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
//object["spaceTimeGUID"] = "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721";
//object["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839873;
object["names"] = {"对象21","对象22"};
//object["guids"] = {"5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f","5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"};
//object["ids"] = {(uint64)158789545685235558,(uint64)158789545685235559};
objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参

// 订阅对象

param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST_UPDATE";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//-指定时空
condition.clear();
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST_UPDATE2";
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; //指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1/cj1/cx1","gc1/cj1/cx2"};
//condition["spaceTimeGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["spaceTimeIDs"] = {(uint64)18158513697557839872,(uint64)18158513697557839873};
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921"; // 模型GUID
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

 4.5.5.2.2. 订阅指定模型的对象 
 // 脚本示例：订阅指定模型的对象的修改事件
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; // 回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
int32[] eventTypes;
stringMap<var> pubConfig; 
//-当前时空/数据区
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST_UPDATE";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::OBJECT_BY_MODEL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; //当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区

condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//-指定时空
condition.clear();
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "SUB_MODEL_OBJECT_LIST_UPDATE2";
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; //指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeNames"] = {"gc1/cj1/cx1","gc1/cj1/cx2"};
//condition["spaceTimeGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["spaceTimeIDs"] = {(uint64)18158513697557839872,(uint64)18158513697557839873};

condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅对象
Result res = Subscribe(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");

}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}
 

# 4.5.5.2.3. 订阅回调

// 订阅功能回调功能入参声明：Dataset callback

int32 rowLen = callback.rowLength; // 数据集总行数
int32 rowNo = 1; // 数据集行号，这里以一行举例，请视实际情况决定要不要循环处理

int32 type = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$type");
int32 eventType = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$eventType");

if(Enum_Rt_Type::TSENTITY == type) //处理单灵敏时序物
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 var value = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$value");
 int32 timeStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$timeStamp");
 int32 qualityStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$qualityStamp");
 var oldvalue = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$old_value");
 int32 oldtimeStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$old_timeStamp");
 int32 oldqualityStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$old_qualityStamp");
 stringMap updateFieldValues = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$updateFieldValues"); //变化的k-v
 if(updateFieldValues.containsKey("成员1") ) //如果变化字段中包含成员1
 {
 var value = updateFieldValues.成员1;
 if(value == 1)
 {
 //业务逻辑
 }
 }
}
else if(Enum_Rt_Type::MTSENTITY == type) //处理多灵敏时序物
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 stringMap updateFieldValues = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$updateFieldValues"); //变化的k-v
 if(updateFieldValues.containsKey("灵敏成员1") ) //如果变化字段中包含灵敏成员1
 {
 int32 timeStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$timeStamp");
 int32 qualityStamp = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$qualityStamp");
 var value = updateFieldValues.灵敏成员1;
 if(value == 1)
 {
 //业务逻辑
 }
 }
 if(updateFieldValues.containsKey("成员1") ) //如果变化字段中包含成员1
 {
 var value = updateFieldValues.成员1;
 if(value == 1)
 {
 //业务逻辑
 }
 }
}
else //处理其他对象
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string name = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string guid = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 stringMap updateFieldValues = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$updateFieldValues"); //变化的k-v
 if(updateFieldValues.containsKey("成员1") ) //如果变化字段中包含成员1
 {
 var value = updateFieldValues.成员1;
 if(value == 1)
 {
 //业务逻辑
 }
 }
}

# 4.6. 记录

## 4.6. 记录

# 4.6.1. 创建记录

// 函数示例：给2个业务事对象各添加2条记录
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
// 入参
stringMap input;
input["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
stringMap [] fieldValues; 
stringMap fieldValue; 
var[][] dValues; 
var[] values;

// 第一个对象
fieldValue["objectName"] = "object1";
//fieldValue["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f");
//fieldValue["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558); 
fieldValue["dataFields"] = {"$parentRecordID","$startTime","mem1","mem2"};

values = {(uint64)20975487412474117,(int64)194547845120000,25.3,166}; //有父记录，父记录必须是父对象的记录
dValues.push(new values); // 第一条记录
values = {(uint64)0,(int64)194547845120000,67.3,201}; //无父记录
dValues.push(new values); // 第二条记录
fieldValue["dataValues"] = dValues;
fieldValues.push(new fieldValue);

// 第二个对象
fieldValue["objectName"] = "object2";
//fieldValue["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//fieldValue["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
fieldValue["dataFields"] = {"$startTime","mem4","mem5"};

values = {(int64)194547845120000,25,16.6};
dValues.clear(); 
dValues.push(new values); // 第一条记录
values = {(int64)194547845120000,67,20.1};
dValues.push(new values); // 第二条记录
fieldValue["dataValues"] = dValues;
fieldValues.push(new fieldValue);

input["fieldValues"] = fieldValues;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 给对象添加多条记录
Result res = Create(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

uint64[] ids = output.ids; // 每条记录的id
int32 [] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每条记录的错误码

### 4.6.1. 创建记录

 // 函数示例：给2个业务事对象各添加2条记录
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
// 入参

input["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
stringMap<var>[] fieldValues; 
stringMap<var> fieldValue; 
var[][] dValues; 
var[] values;

// 第一个对象
fieldValue["objectName"] = "object1";
//fieldValue["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f");
//fieldValue["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558); 
fieldValue["dataFields"] = {"$parentRecordID","$startTime","mem1","mem2"};

values = {(uint64)20975487412474117,(int64)194547845120000,25.3,166}; //有父记录，父记录必须是父对象的记录
dValues.push(new values); // 第一条记录
values = {(uint64)0,(int64)194547845120000,67.3,201}; //无父记录
dValues.push(new values); // 第二条记录
fieldValue["dataValues"] = dValues;
fieldValues.push(new fieldValue);

// 第二个对象
fieldValue["objectName"] = "object2";
//fieldValue["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//fieldValue["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
fieldValue["dataFields"] = {"$startTime","mem4","mem5"};

values = {(int64)194547845120000,25,16.6};
dValues.clear(); 
dValues.push(new values); // 第一条记录
values = {(int64)194547845120000,67,20.1};
dValues.push(new values); // 第二条记录
fieldValue["dataValues"] = dValues;
fieldValues.push(new fieldValue);

input["fieldValues"] = fieldValues;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 给对象添加多条记录
Result res = Create(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

uint64[] ids = output.ids; // 每条记录的id

# 4.6.2. 删除记录

// 示例1：删除指定2个对象下的4条记录
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] reords;
stringMap mReord;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

mReord["objectName"] = "object1";
//mReord["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//mReord["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
mReord["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474117,20975487412474118};
reords.push(new mReord);

mReord["objectName"] = "object2";
//mReord["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//mReord["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
mReord["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474332,20975487412474333};
reords.push(new mReord);
condition["records"] = reords;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 删除对象记录
Result res = Delete(param, input, output);
int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"删除成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"删除失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

### 4.6.2. 删除记录

 // 示例1：删除指定2个对象下的4条记录
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] reords;
stringMap<var> mReord;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

mReord["objectName"] = "object1";
//mReord["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//mReord["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
mReord["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474117,20975487412474118};
reords.push(new mReord);

mReord["objectName"] = "object2";
//mReord["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//mReord["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
mReord["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474332,20975487412474333};
reords.push(new mReord);
condition["records"] = reords;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 删除对象记录
Result res = Delete(param, input, output);
int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"删除成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"删除失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.6.3. 修改记录

### 4.6.3. 修改记录

# 4.6.3.1. 修改指定recordID的记录

// 示例：修改指定2个对象下的4条记录的成员
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] datas;
stringMap mData;
var[][] dValues;
var[] values;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

// 对象1下1条记录
mData["objectName"] = "事对象1";
//mData["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//mData["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
mData["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474116};
mData["dataFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};

values = {12,3.14}; //第1条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
mData["dataValues"] = dValues;
datas.push(new mData);
// 对象2下3条记录
mData["objectName"] = "事对象2";
//mData["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//mData["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
mData["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474117,20975487412474118,20975487412474119};
mData["dataFields"] = {"mem12","mem22"};

values = {100,"已完成"}; // 第1条记录的字段值
dValues.clear();
dValues.push(new values);
values = {200,"已完成"}; // 第2条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
values = {300,"已完成"}; // 第3条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
mData["dataValues"] = dValues;
datas.push(new mData);

condition["datas"] = datas;
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

#### 4.6.3.1. 修改指定recordID的记录

 // 示例：修改指定2个对象下的4条记录的成员
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] datas;
stringMap<var> mData;
var[][] dValues;
var[] values;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

// 对象1下1条记录
mData["objectName"] = "事对象1";
//mData["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//mData["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
mData["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474116};
mData["dataFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};

values = {12,3.14}; //第1条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
mData["dataValues"] = dValues;
datas.push(new mData);
// 对象2下3条记录
mData["objectName"] = "事对象2";
//mData["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//mData["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
mData["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474117,20975487412474118,20975487412474119};
mData["dataFields"] = {"mem12","mem22"};

values = {100,"已完成"}; // 第1条记录的字段值
dValues.clear();
dValues.push(new values);
values = {200,"已完成"}; // 第2条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
values = {300,"已完成"}; // 第3条记录的字段值
dValues.push(new values);
mData["dataValues"] = dValues;
datas.push(new mData);

condition["datas"] = datas;
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.6.3.2. 修改指定对象的记录（仅业务）

// 示例：修改对象下的mem1>50000的记录
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;

//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;

mulFieldValue["mem_leveldesc"] = "高";
mulFieldValue["mem3_level"] = 1;
condition ["mulFieldValue"] = mulFieldValue;
conditions.push(new condition);

// 出参

 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");

 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量

# 4.6.4. 查询记录

### 4.6.4. 查询记录

# 4.6.4.1. 查询指定recordID的记录

// 示例：查询2个对象的6条记录
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
//-查询当前时空/数据区
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["recordIDs"] = {20975487412474117,20975487412474118};
condition["returnFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//-查询指定时空
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object2";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
condition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};
condition["returnFields"] = {"mem11","mem22"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Query(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 int32 mem1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem1");
 float mem2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem2");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 4.6.4.1. 查询指定recordID的记录

# 4.6.4.2. 查询指定对象的记录

// 示例：查询对象的记录
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_OBJECT;
//-查询当前时空/数据区
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 当前时空
//condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 数据区
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//-查询指定时空
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object2";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "69045fb0-7bf9-45b1-89cd-5f808e2fbbe6";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235559;
condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Query(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;

 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号

 float mem2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem2");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

# 4.6.4.3. 查询指定父recordID记录的子记录（仅业务）

stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap startcondition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD;
// 父记录的筛选
startCondition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//startCondition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995"; 
//startCondition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872; 
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectName"] = "object1";
//startCondition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"; 
//startCondition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558; 
startCondition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};

// 查询所有子记录
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_ALL;
condition["filter"] = "$startTime > 2083023580345"; // 过滤条件
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectGUID","$recordID","$name"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询指定模型的子记录
condition.clear();
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_MODEL;
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "mem1 > 100"; // 过滤条件
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectGUID","$recordID","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Query(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;

 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 int32 mem1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem1");
 float mem2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem2");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 4.6.4.3. 查询指定父recordID记录的子记录（仅业务）

 stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var> startcondition;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::CHILD;
// 父记录的筛选
startCondition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
startCondition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
startCondition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//startCondition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995"; 
//startCondition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872; 
startCondition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
startCondition["objectName"] = "object1";
//startCondition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f"; 
//startCondition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558; 
startCondition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};

// 查询所有子记录
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_ALL;
condition["filter"] = "$startTime > 2083023580345"; // 过滤条件
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectGUID","$recordID","$name"};
conditions.push(new condition);

// 查询指定模型的子记录
condition.clear();
condition["startCondition"] = startCondition;
condition["mainMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_MODEL;
condition["modelGUID"] = "898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921";
condition["filter"] = "mem1 > 100"; // 过滤条件
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectGUID","$recordID","$name","mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Query(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;

 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 int32 mem1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem1");
 float mem2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"mem2");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;

 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);

# 4.6.5. 订阅记录

### 4.6.5. 订阅记录

# 4.6.5.1. 订阅记录的创建、删除事件

#### 4.6.5.1. 订阅记录的创建、删除事件

# 4.6.5.1.1. 订阅指定recordID的记录

// 示例：订阅指定recordID的记录的删除事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; //回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap pubConfig; 
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "sub_reords_ets";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
condition["eventTypes"] = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅
Result res = Subscribe(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

# 4.6.5.1.2. 订阅指定对象的记录

// 示例：订阅指定对象的记录的创建、删除事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; //回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap pubConfig; 
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "sub_object_reords_ets";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_OBJECT;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_EVENT_TYPES;
condition["eventTypes"] = {(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE,(int32)Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅
Result res = Subscribe(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
}

# 4.6.5.1.3. 订阅回调

// 订阅功能回调功能入参声明：Dataset callback

int32 rowLen = callback.rowLength; // 数据集总行数
int32 rowNo = 1; // 数据集行号，这里以一行举例，请视实际情况决定要不要循环处理

int32 type = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$type");
int32 eventType = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$eventType");

if(Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string objectName = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string objectGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectGUID");
 uint64 recordID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$recordID");
 var mem1 = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"成员1");
 var mem2 = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"成员2");
 //业务逻辑
}
else if(Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string objectName = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string objectGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectGUID");
 uint64 recordID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$recordID");
 //业务逻辑
}
 

 4.6.5.1.3. 订阅回调 
 // 订阅功能回调功能入参声明：Dataset callback

int32 rowLen = callback.rowLength; // 数据集总行数
int32 rowNo = 1; // 数据集行号，这里以一行举例，请视实际情况决定要不要循环处理

int32 type = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$type");
int32 eventType = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$eventType");

if(Enum_Rt_EventType::CREATE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string objectName = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string objectGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectGUID");
 uint64 recordID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$recordID");
 var mem1 = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"成员1");
 var mem2 = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"成员2");
 //业务逻辑
}
else if(Enum_Rt_EventType::DELETE == eventType)
{
 string spaceTimeGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$spaceTimeGUID");
 string objectName = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string objectGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectGUID");
 uint64 recordID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$recordID");
 //业务逻辑
}
 
 

# 4.6.5.2. 订阅记录的修改事件

#### 4.6.5.2. 订阅记录的修改事件

# 4.6.5.2.1. 订阅指定recordID的记录

// 示例：订阅指定recordID的记录的指定字段的修改事件
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0; // 云ID
param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING_RECORD;
param["callbackFuncName"] = "callBackFunc1"; //回调函数名称
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap pubConfig; 
condition["pubConfig"] = pubConfig; //订阅配置
condition["subscribeName"] = "sub_reords_update";
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 订阅
Result res = Subscribe(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 4.6.5.2.1. 订阅指定recordID的记录 
 // 示例：订阅指定recordID的记录的指定字段的修改事件

param["areaID"] = 0; // 数据区ID

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::RECORD_BY_RECORD_ID_LIST_SINGLE_OBJECT;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)18158513697557839872;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectName"] = "object1";
//condition["objectGUID"] = "5a81d7a1-9f2d-4bce-a21e-76e0f04c588f";
//condition["objectID"] = (uint64)158789545685235558;
condition["recordIDs"] = {(uint64)20975487412474121,(uint64)20975487412474119};
condition["cmdCode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SubCmdCode::SUB_UPDATE_SUB_FIELDS;
condition["subFields"] = {"mem1","mem2"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 订阅
Result res = Subscribe(param, input,output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"订阅成功!","");
 uint64[] subIDs = output.subscribeIDs; // 每个condition的订阅ID
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"订阅失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

string objectName = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
string objectGUID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectGUID");
uint64 recordID = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$recordID ");
stringMap updateFieldValues = callback.cellByName(rowNo,"$updateFieldValues"); //变化的k-v
if(updateFieldValues.containsKey("成员1") ) //如果变化字段中包含成员1
{
 var value = updateFieldValues.成员1;
 if(value == 1)
 {
 //业务逻辑
 }
}

# 4.7. 列表属性

## 4.7. 列表属性

# 4.7.1. 组织岗位列表：（人员）

### 4.7.1. 组织岗位列表：（人员）

# 4.7.1.1. 关联组织岗位

// 示例：给2个人员对象关联组织、岗位
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型：人员对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;
var[][] iValues;
var[] iiValues;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"人员对象1","人员对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$orgPostList"}; // 修改字段：组织岗位列表属性
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加组织岗位
condition["itemFields"] = {"$orgGUID","$postGUID"} ;

// 人员对象1关联2个组织、岗位
iiValues = {"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921","797a2f62-904b-1c33-6ef4-123456621921"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"890a2f83-606u-4f27-7u9h-ftu0b0656347","563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);
// 人员对象2关联2个组织、岗位
iiValues = {"890a2f83-606u-4f27-7u9h-ftu0b0656347","452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453"};
iValues.clear();
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"890a2f83-606u-4f27-7u9h-ftu0b0656347","563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);
int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

#### 4.7.1.1. 关联组织岗位

# 4.7.1.2. 解除关联组织岗位

// 示例：2个人员对象解除关联组织、岗位
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型：人员对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"人员对象1","人员对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$orgPostList"}; // 修改字段：组织岗位列表属性
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::REMOVE; // 移除组织岗位

// 人员对象1解除关联
value["filter"] = "$orgGUID==\"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921\""; //移出某组织的所有岗位
values.push(new value);
// 人员对象2解除关联
value["filter"] = "$orgGUID==\"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921\"||$postGUID in (\"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453\",\"563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876\")"; 
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

#### 4.7.1.2. 解除关联组织岗位

 // 示例：2个人员对象解除关联组织、岗位
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型：人员对象
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;

stringMap<var>[] values;
stringMap<var> value;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"人员对象1","人员对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$orgPostList"}; // 修改字段：组织岗位列表属性
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::REMOVE; // 移除组织岗位

// 人员对象1解除关联
value["filter"] = "$orgGUID==\"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921\""; //移出某组织的所有岗位
values.push(new value);
// 人员对象2解除关联
value["filter"] = "$orgGUID==\"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921\"||$postGUID in (\"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453\",\"563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876\")"; 
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.7.1.3. 查询关联的组织岗位

// 示例：查询人员1在指定组织中担任的岗位，人员2担任指定岗位的组织
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::PERSON; // 数据类型：人员对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] lists;
stringMap list;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_PROPERTY_BY_KEY_LIST; // 查找模式
condition["dataField"] = {"$orgPostList"};

condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 指定时空模式
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

list["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
list["objectName"] = "人员对象11";
list["filter"] = "$orgGUID==\"898a2f82-905b-4c43-8ef9-edb0b0621921\""; //指定组织
lists.push(new list);

list["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
list["objectName"] = "人员对象22";
list["filter"] = "$postGUID in (\"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453\",\"563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876\")"; //指定岗位
lists.push(new list);

condition["lists"] = lists;
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$orgGUID","$postGUID"};

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$orgGUID");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$postGUID");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

 // 示例：查询人员1在指定组织中担任的岗位，人员2担任指定岗位的组织

list["objectName"] = "人员对象11";

lists.push(new list);

list["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
list["objectName"] = "人员对象22";
list["filter"] = "$postGUID in (\"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453\",\"563y7r43-560c-1r55-2y7u-678903345876\")"; //指定岗位
lists.push(new list);

condition["lists"] = lists;
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$orgGUID","$postGUID"};

conditions.push(new condition);

// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$orgGUID");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$postGUID");
}
else
{

 int32[] exErrorCodes;

 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 

# 4.7.2. 外键列表：

### 4.7.2. 外键列表：

# 4.7.2.1. 添加外键

// 示例：给事对象增加外键
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;
var[][] iValues;
var[] iiValues;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$foreignFieldList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加外键
condition["itemFields"] = {"$foreignField","$referenceType","$referenceGUID","$referenceField"} ;

// 业务事对象1添加外键
iiValues = {"成员1",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"890a2f83-606u-4f27-7u9h-ftu0b0656347","f1"};
iValues.clear();
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"成员3",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453","f3"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);
// 业务事对象2添加外键
iiValues = {"成员3",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453","f3"};
iValues.clear();
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

#### 4.7.2.1. 添加外键

 // 示例：给事对象增加外键
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象

condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$foreignFieldList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加外键
condition["itemFields"] = {"$foreignField","$referenceType","$referenceGUID","$referenceField"} ;

// 业务事对象1添加外键
iiValues = {"成员1",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"890a2f83-606u-4f27-7u9h-ftu0b0656347","f1"};
iValues.clear();
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"成员3",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453","f3"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);
// 业务事对象2添加外键
iiValues = {"成员3",Enum_Rt_Type::THING,"452a2f56-374c-1d25-5te3-453215564453","f3"};
iValues.clear();
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{

 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.7.2.2. 删除外键

// 示例：事对象删除外键
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$foreignFieldList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::REMOVE; // 移除外键

// 事对象1移除外键
value["foreignFields"] = {"成员1"};
values.push(new value);
// 事对象2移除外键
value["foreignFields"] = {"成员3"};
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

# 4.7.2.3. 查询外键列表

// 示例：查询指定的业务事对象的外键列表
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST; // 查找模式
condition["dataField"] = {"$foreignFieldList"};

condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象11","业务事对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象21","业务事对象22"};

objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;

condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$foreignField","$referenceGUID","$referenceField"};

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$foreignField");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$referenceGUID");
 string v4 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$referenceField");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 4.7.2.3. 查询外键列表

 // 示例：查询指定的业务事对象的外键列表
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
stringMap<var>[] objects;
stringMap<var> object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST; // 查找模式
condition["dataField"] = {"$foreignFieldList"};

condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象11","业务事对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象21","业务事对象22"};

objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;

condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$foreignField","$referenceGUID","$referenceField"};

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$foreignField");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$referenceGUID");
 string v4 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$referenceField");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}
 

# 4.7.2.4. 查询指定成员的外键信息

condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

list["objectName"] = "业务事对象11";
