# 4.7.3. 唯一索引：

### 4.7.3. 唯一索引：

# 4.7.3.1. 添加唯一索引

// 示例：给事对象增加唯一索引
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;
var[][] iValues;
var[] iiValues;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$uniqueIndexList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加唯一索引
condition["itemFields"] = {"$indexName","$mulMemberName"} ;

// 业务事对象1添加2个唯一索引
iiValues = {"班级姓名","mem_班级,mem_姓名"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"testui","mem3,mem4"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
iValues.clear();
values.push(new value);
// 业务事对象2添加唯一索引
iiValues = {"班级排名","mem_班级,mem_排名"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
iValues.clear();
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

#### 4.7.3.1. 添加唯一索引

 // 示例：给事对象增加唯一索引
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;

stringMap<var>[] values;
stringMap<var> value;
var[][] iValues;
var[] iiValues;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$uniqueIndexList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加唯一索引
condition["itemFields"] = {"$indexName","$mulMemberName"} ;

// 业务事对象1添加2个唯一索引
iiValues = {"班级姓名","mem_班级,mem_姓名"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
iiValues = {"testui","mem3,mem4"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
iValues.clear();
values.push(new value);
// 业务事对象2添加唯一索引
iiValues = {"班级排名","mem_班级,mem_排名"};
iValues.push(new iiValues);
value["itemValues"] = iValues;
iValues.clear();
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.7.3.2. 删除唯一索引

// 示例：事对象删除唯一索引
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;

condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$uniqueIndexList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::REMOVE; // 移除唯一索引

// 事对象1移除唯一索引
value["indexNames"] = {"班级姓名"};
values.push(new value);
// 事对象2移除唯一索引
value["foreignFields"] = {"班级排名"};
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

// 示例：查询指定的业务事对象的唯一索引列表
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] objects;
stringMap object;
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST; // 查找模式
condition["dataField"] = {"$uniqueIndexList"};

condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象11","业务事对象12"};
objects.push(new object);
object["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx2";
object["names"] = {"业务事对象21","业务事对象22"};

objects.push(new object);
condition["objects"] = objects;

condition["filter"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$indexName","$mulMemberName"};

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$indexName");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$mulMemberName");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

# 4.7.3.4. 查询指定索引名称的索引信息

// 示例：查询指定的业务事对象的指定索引名称的索引信息
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
stringMap [] lists;
stringMap list;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_PROPERTY_BY_KEY_LIST; // 查找模式
condition["dataField"] = {"$uniqueIndexList"};

condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME;
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

list["spaceTimeName"] = "gc1/cj1/cx1";
list["objectName"] = "业务事对象11";
list["indexNames"] = {"班级姓名"};
lists.push(new list);

condition["lists"] = lists;
condition["returnFields"] = {"$objectName","$indexName","$mulMemberName"};

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$indexName");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$mulMemberName");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 4.7.3.4. 查询指定索引名称的索引信息

 // 示例：查询指定的业务事对象的指定索引名称的索引信息

condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["objectIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

list["objectName"] = "业务事对象11";
list["indexNames"] = {"班级姓名"};

// 查询

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$objectName");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$indexName");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$mulMemberName");
}
else

# 4.7.4. 普通索引：

### 4.7.4. 普通索引：

# 4.7.4.1. 给模型的对象添加索引

// 示例：给业务物模型的对象添加索引
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY; // 数据类型：业务物对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::INDEX_LIST_BY_MODEL_LIST;
condition["modelGUIDs"] = {"05dd72fb-62b3-48ee-9bed-eacdfd454eed","634de4b2-0624-4ffc-a46e-7ba3a498192f"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加索引

// 模型1对象添加索引
value["memberNames"] = {"mem1","mem3","mem5"};
values.push(new value);
// 模型2对象添加索引
value["memberNames"] = {"mem2","mem6"};
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

# 4.7.4.3. 查询模型的对象的索引

#### 4.7.4.3. 查询模型的对象的索引

# 4.7.4.4. 指定的对象添加索引

// 示例：给事对象增加索引
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::THING; // 数据类型：业务事对象
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;

stringMap [] values;
stringMap value;

condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::LIST_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["names"] = {"业务事对象1","业务事对象2"};
condition["dataField"] = {"$indexList"};
condition["updateMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_UpdateMode::ADD; // 添加索引

// 业务事对象1添加索引
value["memberNames"] = {"mem1","mem3","mem5"};
values.push(new value);
// 业务事对象2添加索引
value["memberNames"] = {"mem2","mem6"};
values.push(new value);

condition["listValues"] = values;

conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 修改对象出参
stringMap output;
// 修改对象
Result res = Update(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap [] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}

// 事对象1移除索引

int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"修改成功!","");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorInfos = output.errorInfos; // 每个condition的错误信息
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 stringMap<var> errorInfo;
 int32 totalCount;
 int32 affectedCount;
 errorInfo = errorInfos[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的错误信息
 totalCount = errorInfo.totalCount; // 定位到的数据数量
 affectedCount = errorInfo.affectedCount; // 受影响的数据数量

 Trace(2,"修改失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
 Trace(2,"errorInfos=",errorInfos);
}
 

# 4.8. 运行拷贝

## 4.8. 运行拷贝

# 4.8.1. 查询：

### 4.8.1. 查询：

# 4.8.1.1. 查询指定的拷贝

// 示例：查询指定的业务物拷贝
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY_COPY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
//查询本时空下指定的拷贝
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
condition["repoGUID"] = ""; 
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)7782220156096218158,(uint64)7782220156096218159};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$modelGUID","$modelVersion"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//查询指定时空下指定的拷贝
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 查找指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "jt1/gc1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)158789545685235556;
condition["repoGUID"] = "";

condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)7782220156096218158,(uint64)7782220156096218159};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$modelGUID","$modelVersion"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$modelGUID");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

// 示例：查询仓库中的业务物拷贝
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY_COPY; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
string[] strarrnull;
int32[] intarrnull;
//查询本时空下的业务物拷贝列表
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_ALL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 时空模式：app本时空
condition["repoGUID"] = "";
condition["modelGUIDs"] = strarrnull;
condition["modelVersions"] = intarrnull;
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$modelGUID","$modelVersion"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//查询指定时空下的业务物拷贝列表
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_ALL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 时空模式：指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;

//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)158789545685235556;
condition["repoGUID"] = "";

condition["modelGUIDs"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
condition["modelVersions"] = {1,1};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$spaceTimeGUID","$guid","$name","$modelGUID","$modelVersion"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参

int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms

// 示例：查询指定的业务物模型
stringMap param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY_MODEL; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap input;
stringMap [] conditions;
stringMap condition;
//查询本时空下指定guid+version的模型
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 查找本时空
condition["repoGUID"] = "";
condition["identifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::GUID;
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)2017612633061983278,(uint64)2017612633061983279};
condition["versions"] = {1,4};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$version"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//查询指定时空下指定id+version的模型
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 查找指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "jt1/gc1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)158789545685235556;
condition["repoGUID"] = "";

//condition["ids"] = {(uint64)2017612633061983278,(uint64)2017612633061983279};
condition["versions"] = {1,1};
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$version"};
conditions.push(new condition);
input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参

// 出参

int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$modelGUID");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

#### 4.9.1.2. 查询模型的列表

 // 示例：查询仓库中的业务物模型
stringMap<var> param;
param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::ENTITY_MODEL; // 数据类型
// 入参
stringMap<var> input;
stringMap<var>[] conditions;
stringMap<var> condition;
//查询本时空下的业务物模型列表
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_ALL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 时空模式：app本时空
condition["repoGUID"] = ""; 
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$version"};
conditions.push(new condition);
//查询指定时空下的业务物模型列表
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::MDATA_ALL;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; // 时空模式：指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "jt1/gc1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)158789545685235556;
condition["repoGUID"] = "";
condition["returnFields"] = {"$guid","$name","$version"};
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;
// 出参
stringMap<var> output;
// 查询
Result res = Query(param, input, output);

int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID
if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 int32 rowNo = 3; // 数据集行号
 string v1 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
 string v2 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 string v3 = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$modelGUID");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap<var>[] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap<var> errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;
 errorCodeEx = errorCodeExs[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件的子错误码
 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;
 
 Trace(2,"查询失败，ret=",ret);
 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
}

# 4.10.1.1. 查询指定的仓库

//示例_查询指定的运行仓库
stringMap param, input, output,condition;
stringMap [] conditions;
Result res;
string[] returnFields;

param["cloudID"] = 0;
param["areaID"] = 0;
param["transactionID"] = (uint64)0;
param["type"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Type::REPO;

returnFields = {"$guid","$name","$packetVersion","$packetDescription","$spaceTimeGUID","$parentGUID","$packetTime","$status"};

//在App部署时空里查询
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::REPO_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::CURRENT_SPACETIME; // 时空选择模式
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
condition["packetVersions"] = {1,3};
condition["returnFields"] = returnFields;
conditions.push(new condition);

//在指定时空里查询
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::REPO_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::SPECIFY_SPACETIME; //时空选择模式，指定时空
condition["spaceTimeIdentifierType"] = (int32)Enum_IdentifierType::NAME;
condition["spaceTimeName"] = "jt1/gc1/cx1";
//condition["spaceTimeGUID"] = "342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995";
//condition["spaceTimeID"] = (uint64)158789545685235556;
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
condition["packetVersions"] = {1,3};
condition["returnFields"] = returnFields;
conditions.push(new condition);

//在数据区里查询
condition.clear();
condition["mode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_Mode::REPO_BY_IDX_LIST;
condition["spaceTimeMode"] = (int32)Enum_Rt_SpaceTimeMode::ALL_SPACETIME; // 时空选择模式
condition["guids"] = {"342406d2-a99d-439b-9c66-8eb6858eb995", "7a8d69b3-30f7-4198-946d-ec3fae8c5721"};
condition["packetVersions"] = {1,3};
condition["returnFields"] = returnFields;
conditions.push(new condition);

input["conditions"] = conditions;

res = Query(param, input, output);
 
int32 ret = res.ret; // 返回结果码
int32 consumeTime = res.consumeTime; // 执行耗时ms
int64 traceID = res.traceID; // 任务跟踪ID

if(0 == ret)
{
 Trace(2,"查询成功!","");
 DataSet[] returnDatas = output.returnDatas; // 每个condition的数据集
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号 
 DataSet dataSetUM;
 string nameI;
 string guidI;
 dataSetUM = returnDatas[condNo]; // 获取第condNo个condition条件查询返回的数据集
 
 nameI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$name");
 guidI = dataSetUM.cellByName(rowNo,"$guid");
}
else
{
 int32[] errorCodes = output.errorCodes; // 每个condition的错误码
 stringMap [] errorCodeExs = output.errorCodeExs; // 每个condition的子错误码
 
 int32 condNo = 1; // 条件序号
 stringMap errorCodeEx;
 int32[] exErrorCodes;

 exErrorCodes = errorCodeEx.errorCodes;

 Trace(2,"errorCodes=",errorCodes);
 Trace(2,"errorCodeExs=",errorCodeExs);
